                  def paginate(patients)

                    page = [ params[:page].to_i, 1 ].max

    133. 
            

            

            
          
      134. 
        
      
      
        
      
          
    134. 
            

            

                    start_index = (page - 1) * per_page

              def rate_info_for(throttle_data, keys, limit, period, now)

              def truncate_text(text, length)
